AUTHOR     (F.E.BERTRAND,R.W.PEELLE)                              O029200100006 
REFERENCE  (R,ORNL-4455,196911)                                   O029200100007

INSTITUTE  (1USAORL)                                              O029200100010 
FACILITY   (ISOCY) Oak Ridge Isochronous Cyclotron.               O029200100011 
           (SPECM) Momentum Analyzed in a 153 Degree Magnet.      O029200100012 
INC-SPECT  .Monoenergetic 28.8 +/- 0.1 and 60.9 to 61.9 +/- 0.1   O029200100013 
            MeV Protons, Focused on the Target in a Spot of       O029200100014 
            Approximately 8 mm Diameter, with a Walk of +/- 0.4   O029200100015 
            Cm. The Uncertainty in Number of Protons Striking the O029200100016 
            Target was +/- 1 %.                                   O029200100017 
METHOD     (EDE) The Secondary Particle Type was Identified with  O029200100018 
           (TOF) A Combination of Delta-E Versus E and Flight-    O029200100019 
            Time Versus E, Which Permitted Unambiguous Identifi-  O029200100020 
            Cation Over the Whole Reported Energy Range. The Low- O029200100021 
            Energy Cutoffs For the Different Particles were       O029200100022 
           -------------------------------------------------------O029200100023 
             61.7 MeV                                             O029200100024 
                  Protons         2.8 -  3.4 MeV                  O029200100025 
                  Deuterons       2.3 -  2.9 MeV                  O029200100026 
                  Tritons         6.2 -  6.6 MeV                  O029200100027 
                  Helium-3        6.6 - 13.1 MeV                  O029200100028 
                  Alphas          2.8 - 14.5 MeV                  O029200100029 
             28.8 MeV                                             O029200100030 
                  Protons                1.8 MeV                  O029200100031 
                  Deuterons              1.7 MeV                  O029200100032 
                  Tritons                6.2 MeV                  O029200100033 
                  Helium-3               6.6 MeV                  O029200100034 
                  Alphas                 2.5 MeV                  O029200100035 
           -------------------------------------------------------O029200100036 
DETECTOR   (TELES,SOLST,GELI) A Solid State Three-Detector        O029200100037 
            Telescope, with Two Silicon Delta-E Detectors and a   O029200100038 
            Lithium-Drifted Germanium Detector Used For Total     O029200100039 
            Energy Absorption. The Total Resolution was           O029200100040 
           Approximately 180 KeV For Most of the Data.            O029200100041 
           For the 61.7 MeV                                       O029200100042 
            Runs, the Telescope was Shielded by Tantalum or NickelO029200100043 
            Collimators, with Thicknesses of 0.432 - 0.653 Cm and O029200100044 
            Areas of 0.183 - 0.522 Cm2 +/- 1.5 %, Placed at       O029200100045 
            Distances from the Target of 45.8 - 46.4 Cm +/- 1%.   O029200100046 
            At 28.8 MeV the Collimator was 0.013 Cm Thick         O029200100047 
            Tantalum with an Opening of 0.522 Cm2 +/- 1.5%,       O029200100048 
            Placed at a Distance of 45.8 Cm +/- 1% from the       O029200100049 
            Target. The Collimator had a Misalignment at the      O029200100050 
            Center of the Scattering Chamber of +/- 0.5 Cm. The   O029200100051 
            Precision of the Detector Angle was +/- 0.5 Degrees.  O029200100052 
            The Zero Angle was Determined to +/- 0.5 Degrees. The O029200100053 
            Angular Resolution was +/- 1.2 Degrees.               O029200100054 
SAMPLE     .Three Different Aluminium Targets were Used, with the O029200100055 
            Following Thicknesses and Nonuniformities,            O029200100056 
               Energy          Thickness       Nonuniformity      O029200100057 
                MeV             Mg/Cm2            Percent         O029200100058 
                61.7         5.20 +/- 0.052       +/- 1.0         O029200100059 
                61.7         3.80 +/- 0.038       +/- 1.0         O029200100060 
             61.7, 28.8      1.23 +/- 0.012       +/- 1.5         O029200100061 
CORRECTION .The Data were Corrected For                           O029200100062 
            1. Nuclear Reactions in the Germanium Detector,       O029200100063 
            2. Dead Layer in the Path of the Scattered Particles, O029200100064 
            3. Multiple Scattering of Particles in the First Two  O029200100065 
               Detectors, Which Made Them Miss the Total Absorp-  O029200100066 
               Tion Detector,                                     O029200100067 
            4. Energy Loss of the Secondary Particles in the      O029200100068 
               Target,                                            O029200100069 
            5. Collimator Misalignment and Beam-Spot Walk, and    O029200100070 
            6. Collimator Edge Penetration by the Scattered       O029200100071 
               Particles.                                         O029200100072
